crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:fn sql_expr_references_only_group_fields(expr: &SqlExpr, group_by: &[String]) -> bool {
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Field(field) => group_by.iter().any(|group_field| group_field == field),
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Aggregate(_) => false,
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Literal(_) | SqlExpr::Param { .. } => true,
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Membership { expr, .. }
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        | SqlExpr::Like { expr, .. }

crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::FunctionCall { args, .. } => args
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:            .all(|arg| sql_expr_references_only_group_fields(arg, group_by)),
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Binary { left, right, .. } => {
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:            sql_expr_references_only_group_fields(left, group_by)

crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Case { arms, else_expr } => {

crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:fn sql_expr_has_direct_field_outside_aggregate(expr: &SqlExpr) -> bool {
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Field(_) => true,
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Aggregate(_) | SqlExpr::Literal(_) | SqlExpr::Param { .. } => false,
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        SqlExpr::Membership { expr, .. }
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        | SqlExpr::Like { expr, .. }
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        | SqlExpr::NullTest { expr, .. }
crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:        | SqlExpr::Unary { expr, .. } => sql_expr_has_direct_field_outside_aggregate(expr),

crates/icydb-core/src/db/session/tests/mod.rs:            sql_expr_has_direct_field_outside_aggregate(left)
